Each piece moves as a rook in Chess, horizontally and vertically.\r\n* A piece cannot move through another piece.\r\n* When a player sandwiches opponent's piece(s) by two of his own pieces, he captures the sandwiched piece(s). A player can sandwich horizontally and vertically, but NOT diagonally.\r\n* A Player wins when the opponent only has 4 or less pieces left on the board.\r\n\r\nFor more details, please see the \"How
